[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack. The overflow was uncovered by a libFuzzer-based harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_ber`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhile processing a malformed or unexpected BER GeneralString input.[0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer identifies a “stack-buffer-overflow” in [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3194:34[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow occurs when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting one byte beyond the bounds of the stack-allocated buffer `name_string` in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe call stack rooted at `try_dissect_unknown_ber`.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability classification  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The flaw is a stack-based buffer overflow, which can lead to corruption of [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39madjacent stack memory. Such vulnerabilities may be exploitable for [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial-of-service or, in some circumstances, arbitrary code execution.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The failing write is at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m of `name_string`, which is defined as [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m160[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m240[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the stack frame[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the code writes just before the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstart of that buffer’s allocated region.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overwritten address lies in the red-zone between local variables, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering a sanitization abort.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack indicates the issue propagates from `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mback through the generic BER-handling routines [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`try_dissect_unknown_ber`, [0m         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3098[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3099[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3100[0m[39m:    return end_offset;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3101[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root‐Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The overflow occurs in dissect_ber_GeneralString [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-ber.[0m[1;92mc:3174[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInstead of using the BER‐decoded length, the code wrongly reads the first content [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte via tvb_get_uint8 and treats it as the string length. If that byte ≥ name_len [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the logic copies up to name_len−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m bytes but then writes the terminator at [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex tvb_len [0m[1;39m([0m[39m≥[0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, overrunning the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m‐byte stack buffer.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The proper pattern, used elsewhere in packet-ber.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissect_ber_constrained_octet_string[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, is to clamp the actual content length to the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer capacity−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m, memcpy exactly that many bytes, then null-terminate at the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclamped index.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Proposed Patch Steps[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. In packet-ber.c, locate dissect_ber_GeneralString [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m3174[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Remove the `int8_t tvb_len;` declaration and all calls to [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Within the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mname_string && out_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` block, replace the existing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“read‐first‐byte” logic with:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Query the actual payload length from `out_tvb`, e.g.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        unsigned data_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Clamp `data_len` to `name_len−[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        unsigned copy_len = data_len >= name_len ? name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : data_len;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Copy exactly `copy_len` bytes:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Null-terminate at `copy_len`:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Ensure all variables use unsigned [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor guint32[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to avoid signed/unsigned [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpitfalls.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Retain the return value and existing functionality of [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissect_ber_restricted_string; only the buffer‐fill logic is altered.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   f. Add a regression unit test [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif not already present[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m feeding a GeneralString [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhose first byte exceeds the buffer size to confirm no overflow and a properly [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated, NUL‐terminated string in `name_string`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The change follows the same approach as other string dissectors in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-ber.c, preserving the intended “read up to the available length but never [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexceed the buffer” behavior.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not modify any fuzz harness or external code; only the in-core BER [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring handler is updated.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The new logic may copy more bytes than the previous “single‐byte length” [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterpretation, but that is correct: the old logic misread the length. In practice,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb` always represents exactly the BER-decoded content, so reading its full [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength gives the intended string content.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is no change to offset arithmetic or downstream protocol tree [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsertion—only local buffering is affected.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By clamping and null-terminating in one place, we remove an entire class of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds writes. Standard buffer‐overflow tests for other BER string types [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould pass unchanged.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Broader Audit[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After patching GeneralString, audit IA5String, UTF8String, GraphicString, and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother restricted‐string dissectors for similar misuse of first‐byte–as–length [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that all tvb_memcpy calls in packet-ber.c follow the “length clamp + [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnull-terminate” pattern seen in dissect_ber_constrained_octet_string.[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
